 Stephen's is one of the three early colleges that formed the University of Delhi (DU)
 isane chandani chowk main ek kiraaye ke makaan main mahaj paanch chaatro se apana shaikshanik safar shuru kiya tha
 St
 Stephens, started as a high school of a Christian mission, became a college in 1881 and today has developed into a top educational institution in India
 itane varshon ke dauraan isane apni aisi pratishtha banaai he ki desh ke har kone se pratibhavan chaatr isaki taraf khinche chale aate hai
 The college started with just seven subjects, including Philosophy, Sanskrit and English
 dhire-dhire yah fehrist badhati gai or philhal saint stephens angreji, darshanashastra, arthshaastra, itihaas, sanskrit, bie program, bhautikashastra, rasayanashastra, ganit, bhautik vigyaan or computer vigyaan main 11 undergraduate degree course kii peshkash karata he
 From here, especially from the stream of arts, the students who have passed out are more inclined to go into administrative or government service or to earn a name in the sports world
 yahaan ke kaamyaab chaatro kaa doosraa samooh unka he jo macinse and company sareekhe duniya bhar main pratishthit sansthaanon main naukari pate hai
 The first-year students gather at Stephens every morning
 iske vishaal daravaajon se bheetar daakhil hote hi ehsaas hota he ki yahaan sab kuch juda he, kam se kam naam se to he hi
 The hostels at Stephens are called residences or accommodation and the teachers and students are senior members and junior members respectively, the mess is the dining hall and the canteen cafe
 yahi nahin, nivartmaan yaa baahar jane vaale chaatro ke liye yojit vidaai samaaroh ko "dismisal sarvice'' kaha jaataa he

 Hindi day is celebrated every year on 14 September
 bataa den ki hindi sabase pracheen or ek saral bhashaa he
 Today a large number of people have given Hindi a special place in their smartphones
 ab hindi main typing ke liye aapako phone main koi alag ap daalane kii jarurat nahin he
 Hindi typing feature is already present in your phone and computer
 kai log hindi main tip karne ke liye bade sies ke ap downlod kar lete hai jo adhik maatra main phone kii internal memory kaa istemaal karte hai
 By the way, the Hindi keyboard already has inbuilt feature in computers and phones
 bas ise setting main jaakar on karne kii jarurat hoti he
 Learn how, by setting Hindi in your mobile keyboard, you can also make Hindi a special part of your phone
 google aise detaa he suvidhagugle ke android oparating system par chalane vaale adhiktar phonon main google keyboard pehle hi install rahata he
 The Hindi keyboard is also inbuilt in this keyboard
 is ap main vishwa kii kai anya bhashaaen bhi shaamil hai
 Despite this, many users install different applications for Hindi typing in the phone
 iske liye sabase pehle jis phone main hindi typing karnaa chaahate hai usamen massej kholen
 Then in the given typing option, a globe will appear on the top or bottom of the keyboard
 aapako isi nishaan par clic karnaa he
 Clicking on it will open many options including Hindi on the phone screen
 isamen se hindi kaa chunaav karen
 By doing this, users can enjoy Hindi typing
 phir hindi se dobaaraa angreji karne ke liye dobaaraa se phir usee iken kaa istemaal karen
 This is also a way to change the keyboard
 If your smartphone does not see the globe icon in the keyboard, do not worry
 iske liye setting main jaaen usamen maujuud Language & Input ke vikalp par clic karen
 This is where you will see default written under the keyboard and input method
 difolt main us ap kaa naam aayega jo aapke phone main vartmaan samay main kaam kar rahaa he
 To activate the feature of Hindi keyboard here, remember that Google keyboard must be in default
 ab dikhegaa Google keyboarddipoylta ke neeche google keyboard dikhaai degaa
 Touching on the right side of that option will open a new display above which Google Keyboard Setting will appear
 yahaan Language vaale box par clic karte hi ek box khul jayega
 a mark will appear in the box, which you have to remove
 is tarah aapaki disple par vishwa kii adhiktar bhashaaon kaa vikalp dikhne lagegaa
 To turn on this Hindi keyboard, going to the bottom, the Hindi option will appear, click on the box to the right of it
 iske saath hi angreji (bharat) vaale box par clic rahane den taaki aap hindi or angreji typing kaa istemaal kar saken
 By adopting this procedure, both Hindi and English options will come in the phone keyboard
 angreji se badal sakate hai hindicomputer main microsoft kii ore se inbilt keyboard kaa sabase bada phayda ye he ki ise hindi or angreji main badalakar likhnaa kaaphi aasaan hota he
 For this, all you have to do is press the Shift + Alt button simultaneously
 udhaaharan ke taur par agar aap hindi typing kar rahe hai to shift+alt ko dabaakar keyboard ko angreji main badal sakate hai
 Then if you are typing in English, you can start typing in Hindi by pressing Shift + Alt button simultaneously
 smart phone yaa computer par hindi likhnaa kaaphi aasaan ho gaya he
